  stree proposal:  0.4000 for Ssnl, 0.6000 for Sspr
    sp: number of delimited specices
    np: number of parameters
  mldp: most likelely delimitation and probability
mthet1: root node mean theta
 mtau1: root node mean tau
log-PG: log-probability of gene trees (MSC)
 log-L: mean log-L of observing data
